		bool c8 = std::find(std::begin(vaxmonth), std::end(vaxmonth), 8) != std::end(vaxmonth); 
		bool c9 = std::find(std::begin(vaxmonth), std::end(vaxmonth), 9) != std::end(vaxmonth); 
		bool c10 = std::find(std::begin(vaxmonth), std::end(vaxmonth), 10) != std::end(vaxmonth); 
		bool c11 = std::find(std::begin(vaxmonth), std::end(vaxmonth), 11) != std::end(vaxmonth); 
		bool c12 = std::find(std::begin(vaxmonth), std::end(vaxmonth), 12) != std::end(vaxmonth); 
		double totdays = (c1*31.0) + (c2*28.0) + (c3*31.0) + (c4*30.0) + (c5*31.0) + (c6*30.0) + 
			(c7*31.0) + (c8*31.0) + (c9*30.0) + (c10*31.0) + (c11*30.0) + (c12*31.0); 

		int tt = int(t); 

		if ((t > tf-(365*10)) && 
			((c1 && tt % 365 >= 1 && tt % 365 < 32) || (c2 && tt % 365 >= 32 && tt % 365 < 60) ||
			(c3 && tt % 365 >= 60 && tt % 365 < 91) || (c4 && tt % 365 >= 91 && tt % 365 < 121) ||
			(c5 && tt % 365 >= 121 && tt % 365 < 152) || (c6 && tt % 365 >= 152 && tt % 365 < 182) ||
			(c7 && tt % 365 >= 182 && tt % 365 < 213) || (c8 && tt % 365 >= 213 && tt % 365 < 244) ||
			(c9 && tt % 365 >= 244 && tt % 365 < 274) || (c10 && tt % 365 >= 274 && tt % 365 < 305) ||
			(c11 && tt % 365 >= 305 && tt % 365 < 335) || (c12 && tt % 365 >= 335 && tt % 365 <= 365)) 
			) {
				
			double today_doses = N * n_vax / totdays;
			Pdg = today_doses;

			double vS_0s = std::min(S_0s, today_doses*vaxgroup[0]*S_0s/(S_0s+R1_0s+R2_0s+R3_0s+RR1_0s+RR2_0s+RR3_0s+RRR1_0s+RRR2_0s+RRR3_0s+RRRR1_0s+RRRR2_0s+RRRR3_0s));
			double vR1_0s = std::min(R1_0s, today_doses*vaxgroup[0]*R1_0s/(S_0s+R1_0s+R2_0s+R3_0s+RR1_0s+RR2_0s+RR3_0s+RRR1_0s+RRR2_0s+RRR3_0s+RRRR1_0s+RRRR2_0s+RRRR3_0s)); 
			double vR2_0s = std::min(R2_0s, today_doses*vaxgroup[0]*R2_0s/(S_0s+R1_0s+R2_0s+R3_0s+RR1_0s+RR2_0s+RR3_0s+RRR1_0s+RRR2_0s+RRR3_0s+RRRR1_0s+RRRR2_0s+RRRR3_0s)); 
			double vR3_0s = std::min(R3_0s, today_doses*vaxgroup[0]*R3_0s/(S_0s+R1_0s+R2_0s+R3_0s+RR1_0s+RR2_0s+RR3_0s+RRR1_0s+RRR2_0s+RRR3_0s+RRRR1_0s+RRRR2_0s+RRRR3_0s)); 
			double vRR1_0s = std::min(RR1_0s, today_doses*vaxgroup[0]*RR1_0s/(S_0s+R1_0s+R2_0s+R3_0s+RR1_0s+RR2_0s+RR3_0s+RRR1_0s+RRR2_0s+RRR3_0s+RRRR1_0s+RRRR2_0s+RRRR3_0s)); 
			double vRR2_0s = std::min(RR2_0s, today_doses*vaxgroup[0]*RR2_0s/(S_0s+R1_0s+R2_0s+R3_0s+RR1_0s+RR2_0s+RR3_0s+RRR1_0s+RRR2_0s+RRR3_0s+RRRR1_0s+RRRR2_0s+RRRR3_0s)); 
			double vRR3_0s = std::min(RR3_0s, today_doses*vaxgroup[0]*RR3_0s/(S_0s+R1_0s+R2_0s+R3_0s+RR1_0s+RR2_0s+RR3_0s+RRR1_0s+RRR2_0s+RRR3_0s+RRRR1_0s+RRRR2_0s+RRRR3_0s)); 
			double vRRR1_0s = std::min(RRR1_0s, today_doses*vaxgroup[0]*RRR1_0s/(S_0s+R1_0s+R2_0s+R3_0s+RR1_0s+RR2_0s+RR3_0s+RRR1_0s+RRR2_0s+RRR3_0s+RRRR1_0s+RRRR2_0s+RRRR3_0s));
